of the overlap is $BD \times \frac{A'C}{AC} = 3 \times \frac{2}{4} = 1.5$. The area of the shaded rhombus is therefore $\frac{1}{2} \times 2 \times 1.5 = 1.5$. Step 4 [Final Conclusion]: \boxed{1.5}
